I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
A std::vector of std::unique_ptrs can't be added
 * Compiler Used: VS2013 (MSVC 12) with ChaiScript v5.8.6
 * Operating System: Windows 10
 * Architecture (ARM/x86/32bit/64bit/etc):  64bit
 

### Expected Behavior 

Being able to successfully compile the following line:

```cpp
struct Foo {};
chai->add(chaiscript::bootstrap::standard_library::vector_type<std::vector<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>>("Foo"));
```

### Actual Behavior 

The compiler error is

```Error  1  error C2280:
std::unique_ptr<Foo,std::default_delete<_Ty>>::unique_ptr(const
std::unique_ptr<_Ty,std::default_delete<_Ty>> &)' : attempting to reference a
deleted function  c:\program files (x86)\microsoft visual studio
12.0\vc\include\vector  1708

```

### Minimal Example to Reproduce Behavior

```cpp
#include <chaiscript/chaiscript.hpp>
#include <chaiscript/chaiscript_stdlib.hpp>
#include <vector>


int main() {
  chaiscript::ChaiScript chai;
   struct Foo {};
   chai.add(chaiscript::bootstrap::standard_library::vector_type<std::vector<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>>("Foo"));
}
```

### Workaround

I went through and identified the bits that caused the compiler to generate a call to the copy constructor of the unique_ptr and commented them out, and got it to compile. ~~Haven't tested actually using the pointers in chai much, but operator[] doesn't work on the unique_ptr vectors with my hack, so its a weak workaround.~~ Using the updated code where I consume the module I create with the hacky extracted code, I'm able to use vectors of unique_ptrs, so that's good.

 [Copy and pasted from here](https://github.com/ChaiScript/ChaiScript/blob/50ca037da95399a3f88b416288e8d111caa24e32/include/chaiscript/dispatchkit/bootstrap_stl.hpp#L487) got turned into this:

```cpp
template <typename VectorType>
chaiscript::ModulePtr register_vector_of_unique_ptr(const std::string& type)
{

    using namespace chaiscript;
    ModulePtr m = std::make_shared<Module>();
    m->add(user_type<VectorType>(), type);

    typedef VectorType::reference(VectorType::*frontptr)();
    typedef VectorType::const_reference(VectorType::*constfrontptr)() const;

    m->add(fun(static_cast<frontptr>(&VectorType::front)), "front");
    m->add(fun(static_cast<constfrontptr>(&VectorType::front)), "front");


    //bootstrap::standard_library::back_insertion_sequence_type<VectorType>(type, m); //breaks unique_ptrs
    //bootstrap::standard_library::sequence_type<VectorType>(type, m); //breaks unique_ptrs
    bootstrap::standard_library::random_access_container_type<VectorType>(type, m);
    bootstrap::standard_library::container_type<VectorType>(type, m);
    bootstrap::standard_library::default_constructible_type<VectorType>(type, m);
    //bootstrap::standard_library::assignable_type<VectorType>(type, m); //breaks unique_ptrs
    bootstrap::standard_library::input_range_type<VectorType>(type, m);

    if (typeid(VectorType) == typeid(std::vector<Boxed_Value>))
    {
        m->eval(R"(
                    def Vector::`==`(Vector rhs) {
                       if ( rhs.size() != this.size() ) {
                         return false;
                       } else {
                         auto r1 = range(this);
                         auto r2 = range(rhs);
                         while (!r1.empty())
                         {
                           if (!eq(r1.front(), r2.front()))
                           {
                             return false;
                           }
                           r1.pop_front();
                           r2.pop_front();
                         }
                         true;
                       }
                   } )"
                   );
    }

  return m;
}

//elsewhere, make sure to consume the module ptr
chai_instance->add(register_vector_of_unique_ptr<CustomVecOfUniqPtrs>(chai_instance));
```



</pr_description>

    32	namespace chaiscript::bootstrap::standard_library {
    33	  /// Bidir_Range, based on the D concept of ranges.
    34	  /// \todo Update the Range code to base its capabilities on
    35	  ///       the user_typetraits of the iterator passed in
    36	  template<typename Container, typename IterType>
    37	  struct Bidir_Range {
    38	    using container_type = Container;
    39	
    40	    constexpr Bidir_Range(Container &c)
    41	        : m_begin(c.begin())
    42	        , m_end(c.end()) {
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    constexpr bool empty() const noexcept { return m_begin == m_end; }
    46	
    47	    constexpr void pop_front() {
    48	      if (empty()) {
    49	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    50	      }
    51	      ++m_begin;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    constexpr void pop_back() {
    55	      if (empty()) {
    56	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    57	      }
    58	      --m_end;
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    constexpr decltype(auto) front() const {
    62	      if (empty()) {
    63	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    64	      }
    65	      return (*m_begin);
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    constexpr decltype(auto) back() const {
    69	      if (empty()) {
    70	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    71	      }
    72	      auto pos = m_end;
    73	      --pos;
    74	      return (*(pos));
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    IterType m_begin;
    78	    IterType m_end;
    79	  };
    80	
    81	  namespace detail {
    82	    template<typename T>
    83	    size_t count(const T &t_target, const typename T::key_type &t_key) {
    84	      return t_target.count(t_key);
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    template<typename T>
    88	    void insert(T &t_target, const T &t_other) {
    89	      t_target.insert(t_other.begin(), t_other.end());
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    template<typename T>
    93	    void insert_ref(T &t_target, const typename T::value_type &t_val) {
    94	      t_target.insert(t_val);
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    /// Add Bidir_Range support for the given ContainerType
    98	    template<typename Bidir_Type>
    99	    void input_range_type_impl(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
   100	      m.add(user_type<Bidir_Type>(), type + "_Range");
   101	
   102	      copy_constructor<Bidir_Type>(type + "_Range", m);
   103	
   104	      m.add(constructor<Bidir_Type(typename Bidir_Type::container_type &)>(), "range_internal");
   105	
   106	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::empty), "empty");
   107	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::pop_front), "pop_front");
   108	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::front), "front");
   109	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::pop_back), "pop_back");
   110	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::back), "back");
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    /// Algorithm for inserting at a specific position into a container
   114	    template<typename Type>
   115	    void insert_at(Type &container, int pos, const typename Type::value_type &v) {
   116	      auto itr = container.begin();
   117	      auto end = container.end();
   118	
   119	      if (pos < 0 || std::distance(itr, end) < pos) {
   120	        throw std::range_error("Cannot insert past end of range");
   121	      }
   122	
   123	      std::advance(itr, pos);
   124	      container.insert(itr, v);
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    /// Algorithm for erasing a specific position from a container
   128	    template<typename Type>
   129	    void erase_at(Type &container, int pos) {
   130	      auto itr = container.begin();
   131	      auto end = container.end();
   132	
   133	      if (pos < 0 || std::distance(itr, end) <= pos) {
   134	        throw std::range_error("Cannot erase past end of range");
   135	      }
   136	
   137	      std::advance(itr, pos);
   138	      container.erase(itr);
   139	    }
   140	  } // namespace detail
   141	
   142	  template<typename ContainerType>
   143	  void input_range_type(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
   144	    detail::input_range_type_impl<Bidir_Range<ContainerType, typename ContainerType::iterator>>(type, m);
   145	    detail::input_range_type_impl<Bidir_Range<const ContainerType, typename ContainerType::const_iterator>>("Const_" + type, m);
   146	  }

   148	  /// Add random_access_container concept to the given ContainerType
   149	  /// http://www.sgi.com/tech/stl/RandomAccessContainer.html
   150	  template<typename ContainerType>
   151	  void random_access_container_type(const std::string & /*type*/, Module &m) {
   152	    // In the interest of runtime safety for the m, we prefer the at() method for [] access,
   153	    // to throw an exception in an out of bounds condition.
   154	    m.add(fun([](ContainerType &c, int index) -> typename ContainerType::reference {
   155	            /// \todo we are preferring to keep the key as 'int' to avoid runtime conversions
   156	            /// during dispatch. reevaluate
   157	            return c.at(static_cast<typename ContainerType::size_type>(index));
   158	          }),
   159	          "[]");
   160	
   161	    m.add(fun([](const ContainerType &c, int index) -> typename ContainerType::const_reference {
   162	            /// \todo we are preferring to keep the key as 'int' to avoid runtime conversions
   163	            /// during dispatch. reevaluate
   164	            return c.at(static_cast<typename ContainerType::size_type>(index));
   165	          }),
   166	          "[]");
   167	  }

   173	    copy_constructor<ContainerType>(type, m);

   193	    m.add(fun([](const ContainerType *a) { return a->capacity(); }), "capacity");

   213	  /// http://www.sgi.com/tech/stl/Sequence.html
   214	  template<typename ContainerType>
   215	  void sequence_type(const std::string & /*type*/, Module &m) {
   216	    m.add(fun(&detail::insert_at<ContainerType>), []() -> std::string {
   217	      if (typeid(typename ContainerType::value_type) == typeid(Boxed_Value)) {
   218	        return "insert_ref_at";
   219	      } else {
   220	        return "insert_at";
   221	      }
   222	    }());
   223

   225	  }

   227	  /// Add back insertion sequence concept to the given ContainerType
   228	  /// http://www.sgi.com/tech/stl/BackInsertionSequence.html
   229	  template<typename ContainerType>
   230	  void back_insertion_sequence_type(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
   231	    m.add(fun([](ContainerType &container) -> decltype(auto) {
   232	            if (container.empty()) {
   233	              throw std::range_error("Container empty");
   234	            } else {
   235	              return (container.back());
   236	            }
   237	          }),
   238	          "back");
   239	    m.add(fun([](const ContainerType &container) -> decltype(auto) {
   240	            if (container.empty()) {
   241	              throw std::range_error("Container empty");
   242	            } else {
   243	              return (container.back());
   244	            }
   245	          }),
   246	          "back");
   247	
   248	    using push_back = void (ContainerType::*)(const typename ContainerType::value_type &);
   249	    m.add(fun(static_cast<push_back>(&ContainerType::push_back)), [&]() -> std::string {
   250	      if (typeid(typename ContainerType::value_type) == typeid(Boxed_Value)) {
   251	        m.eval("# Pushes the second value onto the container while making a clone of the value\n"
   252	               "def push_back("
   253	               + type
   254	               + " container, x)\n"
   255	                 "{ \n"
   256	                 "  if (x.is_var_return_value()) {\n"
   257	                 "    x.reset_var_return_value() \n"
   258	                 "    container.push_back_ref(x) \n"
   259	                 "  } else { \n"
   260	                 "    container.push_back_ref(clone(x)); \n"
   261	                 "  }\n"
   262	                 "} \n");
   263	
   264	        return "push_back_ref";
   265	      } else {
   266	        return "push_back";
   267	      }
   268	    }());

   270	    m.add(fun(&ContainerType::pop_back), "pop_back");
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  /// Front insertion sequence
   274	  /// http://www.sgi.com/tech/stl/FrontInsertionSequence.html
   275	  template<typename ContainerType>
   276	  void front_insertion_sequence_type(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
   277	    using push_ptr = void (ContainerType::*)(typename ContainerType::const_reference);
   278	    using pop_ptr = void (ContainerType::*)();
   279	
   280	    m.add(fun([](ContainerType &container) -> decltype(auto) {
   281	            if (container.empty()) {
   282	              throw std::range_error("Container empty");
   283	            } else {
   284	              return (container.front());
   285	            }
   286	          }),
   287	          "front");
   288	
   289	    m.add(fun([](const ContainerType &container) -> decltype(auto) {
   290	            if (container.empty()) {
   291	              throw std::range_error("Container empty");
   292	            } else {
   293	              return (container.front());
   294	            }
   295	          }),
   296	          "front");
   297	
   298	    m.add(fun(static_cast<push_ptr>(&ContainerType::push_front)), [&]() -> std::string {
   299	      if (typeid(typename ContainerType::value_type) == typeid(Boxed_Value)) {
   300	        m.eval("# Pushes the second value onto the front of container while making a clone of the value\n"
   301	               "def push_front("
   302	               + type
   303	               + " container, x)\n"
   304	                 "{ \n"
   305	                 "  if (x.is_var_return_value()) {\n"
   306	                 "    x.reset_var_return_value() \n"
   307	                 "    container.push_front_ref(x) \n"
   308	                 "  } else { \n"
   309	                 "    container.push_front_ref(clone(x)); \n"
   310	                 "  }\n"
   311	                 "} \n");
   312	        return "push_front_ref";
   313	      } else {
   314	        return "push_front";
   315	      }
   316	    }());
   317	
   318	    m.add(fun(static_cast<pop_ptr>(&ContainerType::pop_front)), "pop_front");
   319	  }

    18	  template<typename T, typename = typename std::enable_if<std::is_array<T>::value>::type>
    19	  void array(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    20	    using ReturnType = typename std::remove_extent<T>::type;
    21	
    22	    m.add(user_type<T>(), type);
    23	    m.add(fun([](T &t, size_t index) -> ReturnType & {
    24	            constexpr const auto extent = std::extent<T>::value;
    25	            if (extent > 0 && index >= extent) {
    26	              throw std::range_error("Array index out of range. Received: " + std::to_string(index) + " expected < "
    27	                                     + std::to_string(extent));
    28	            } else {
    29	              return t[index];
    30	            }
    31	          }),
    32	          "[]");
    33	
    34	    m.add(fun([](const T &t, size_t index) -> const ReturnType & {
    35	            constexpr const auto extent = std::extent<T>::value;
    36	            if (extent > 0 && index >= extent) {
    37	              throw std::range_error("Array index out of range. Received: " + std::to_string(index) + " expected < "
    38	                                     + std::to_string(extent));
    39	            } else {
    40	              return t[index];
    41	            }
    42	          }),
    43	          "[]");
    44	
    45	    m.add(fun([](const T &) { return std::extent<T>::value; }), "size");
    46	  }
    47	
    48	  /// \brief Adds a copy constructor for the given type to the given Model
    49	  /// \param[in] type The name of the type. The copy constructor will be named "type".
    50	  /// \param[in,out] m The Module to add the copy constructor to
    51	  /// \tparam T The type to add a copy constructor for
    52	  /// \returns The passed in Module
    53	  template<typename T>
    54	  void copy_constructor(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    55	    m.add(constructor<T(const T &)>(), type);
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  /// \brief Add all comparison operators for the templated type. Used during bootstrap, also available to users.
    59	  /// \tparam T Type to create comparison operators for
    60	  /// \param[in,out] m module to add comparison operators to
    61	  /// \returns the passed in Module.
    62	  template<typename T>
    63	  void opers_comparison(Module &m) {
    64	    operators::equal<T>(m);
    65	    operators::greater_than<T>(m);
    66	    operators::greater_than_equal<T>(m);
    67	    operators::less_than<T>(m);
    68	    operators::less_than_equal<T>(m);
    69	    operators::not_equal<T>(m);
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  /// \brief Adds default and copy constructors for the given type
    73	  /// \param[in] type The name of the type to add the constructors for.
    74	  /// \param[in,out] m The Module to add the basic constructors to
    75	  /// \tparam T Type to generate basic constructors for
    76	  /// \returns The passed in Module
    77	  /// \sa copy_constructor
    78	  /// \sa constructor
    79	  template<typename T>
    80	  void basic_constructors(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    81	    m.add(constructor<T()>(), type);
    82	    copy_constructor<T>(type, m);
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  /// \brief Adds a constructor for a POD type
    86	  /// \tparam T The type to add the constructor for
    87	  /// \param[in] type The name of the type
    88	  /// \param[in,out] m The Module to add the constructor to
    89	  template<typename T>
    90	  void construct_pod(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    91	    m.add(fun([](const Boxed_Number &bn) { return bn.get_as<T>(); }), type);
    92	  }
    93	
    94	  /// Internal function for converting from a string to a value
    95	  /// uses ostream operator >> to perform the conversion
    96	  template<typename Input>
    97	  Input parse_string(const std::string &i) {
    98	    if constexpr (!std::is_same<Input, wchar_t>::value && !std::is_same<Input, char16_t>::value && !std::is_same<Input, char32_t>::value) {
    99	      std::stringstream ss(i);
   100	      Input t;
   101	      ss >> t;
   102	      return t;
   103	    } else {
   104	      throw std::runtime_error("Parsing of wide characters is not yet supported");
   105	    }
   106	  }
   107	
   108	  /// Add all common functions for a POD type. All operators, and
   109	  /// common conversions
   110	  template<typename T>
   111	  void bootstrap_pod_type(const std::string &name, Module &m) {
   112	    m.add(user_type<T>(), name);
   113	    m.add(constructor<T()>(), name);
   114	    construct_pod<T>(name, m);
   115	
   116	    m.add(fun(&parse_string<T>), "to_" + name);
   117	    m.add(fun([](const T t) { return t; }), "to_" + name);
   118	    m.add(fun([](const Boxed_Number &bn) { return bn.get_as<T>(); }), "to_" + name);
   119	    m.add(fun(&parse_string<T>), name);
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  /// "clone" function for a shared_ptr type. This is used in the case
   123	  /// where you do not want to make a deep copy of an object during cloning
   124	  /// but want to instead maintain the shared_ptr. It is needed internally
   125	  /// for handling of Proxy_Function object (that is,
   126	  /// function variables.
   127	  template<typename Type>
   128	  auto shared_ptr_clone(const std::shared_ptr<Type> &p) {
   129	    return p;
   130	  }
   131	
   132	  /// Specific version of shared_ptr_clone just for Proxy_Functions
   133	  template<typename Type>
   134	  std::shared_ptr<std::remove_const_t<Type>> shared_ptr_unconst_clone(const std::shared_ptr<std::add_const_t<Type>> &p) {
   135	    return std::const_pointer_cast<typename std::remove_const<Type>::type>(p);
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  /// Assignment function for shared_ptr objects, does not perform a copy of the
   139	  /// object pointed to, instead maintains the shared_ptr concept.
   140	  /// Similar to shared_ptr_clone. Used for Proxy_Function.
   141	  template<typename Type>
   142	  Boxed_Value ptr_assign(Boxed_Value lhs, const std::shared_ptr<Type> &rhs) {
   143	    if (lhs.is_undef() || (!lhs.get_type_info().is_const() && lhs.get_type_info().bare_equal(chaiscript::detail::Get_Type_Info<Type>::get()))) {
   144	      lhs.assign(Boxed_Value(rhs));
   145	      return lhs;
   146	    } else {
   147	      throw exception::bad_boxed_cast("type mismatch in pointer assignment");
   148	    }
   149	  }

   205	    /// Create a bound function object. The first param is the function to bind
   206	    /// the remaining parameters are the args to bind into the result
   207	    static Boxed_Value bind_function(const Function_Params &params) {
   208	      if (params.empty()) {
   209	        throw exception::arity_error(0, 1);
   210	      }
   211	
   212	      Const_Proxy_Function f = boxed_cast<Const_Proxy_Function>(params[0]);
   213	
   214	      if (f->get_arity() != -1 && size_t(f->get_arity()) != params.size() - 1) {
   215	        throw exception::arity_error(static_cast<int>(params.size()), f->get_arity());
   216	      }
   217	
   218	      return Boxed_Value(Const_Proxy_Function(
   219	          std::make_shared<dispatch::Bound_Function>(std::move(f), std::vector<Boxed_Value>(params.begin() + 1, params.end()))));
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    static bool has_guard(const Const_Proxy_Function &t_pf) noexcept {
   223	      auto pf = std::dynamic_pointer_cast<const dispatch::Dynamic_Proxy_Function>(t_pf);
   224	      return pf && pf->has_guard();
   225	    }
   226	
   227	    static Const_Proxy_Function get_guard(const Const_Proxy_Function &t_pf) {
   228	      const auto pf = std::dynamic_pointer_cast<const dispatch::Dynamic_Proxy_Function>(t_pf);
   229	      if (pf && pf->get_guard()) {
   230	        return pf->get_guard();
   231	      } else {
   232	        throw std::runtime_error("Function does not have a guard");
   233	      }
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    template<typename FunctionType>
   237	    static std::vector<Boxed_Value> do_return_boxed_value_vector(FunctionType f, const dispatch::Proxy_Function_Base *b) {
   238	      auto v = (b->*f)();
   239	
   240	      std::vector<Boxed_Value> vbv;
   241	
   242	      for (const auto &o : v) {
   243	        vbv.push_back(const_var(o));
   244	      }
   245	
   246	      return vbv;
   247	    }

   249	    static bool has_parse_tree(const chaiscript::Const_Proxy_Function &t_pf) noexcept {
   250	      const auto pf = std::dynamic_pointer_cast<const chaiscript::dispatch::Dynamic_Proxy_Function>(t_pf);
   251	      return bool(pf);

   254	    static const chaiscript::AST_Node &get_parse_tree(const chaiscript::Const_Proxy_Function &t_pf) {

   256	      if (pf) {

   259	        throw std::runtime_error("Function does not have a parse tree");
   260	      }
   261	    }

    13	#include "proxy_functions.hpp"
    14	
    15	namespace chaiscript::dispatch::detail {
    16	  template<typename Class, typename... Params>
    17	  Proxy_Function build_constructor_(Class (*)(Params...)) {
    18	    if constexpr (!std::is_copy_constructible_v<Class>) {
    19	      auto call = [](auto &&...param) { return std::make_shared<Class>(std::forward<decltype(param)>(param)...); };
    20	
    21	      return Proxy_Function(
    22	          chaiscript::make_shared<dispatch::Proxy_Function_Base,
    23	                                  dispatch::Proxy_Function_Callable_Impl<std::shared_ptr<Class>(Params...), decltype(call)>>(call));
    24	    } else if constexpr (true) {
    25	      auto call = [](auto &&...param) { return Class(std::forward<decltype(param)>(param)...); };
    26	
    27	      return Proxy_Function(
    28	          chaiscript::make_shared<dispatch::Proxy_Function_Base, dispatch::Proxy_Function_Callable_Impl<Class(Params...), decltype(call)>>(
    29	              call));
    30	    }
    31	  }
    32	} // namespace chaiscript::dispatch::detail
    33	
    34	namespace chaiscript {
    35	  /// \brief Generates a constructor function for use with ChaiScript
    36	  ///
    37	  /// \tparam T The signature of the constructor to generate. In the form of: ClassType (ParamType1, ParamType2, ...)
    38	  ///
    39	  /// Example:
    40	  /// \code
    41	  ///    chaiscript::ChaiScript chai;
    42	  ///    // Create a new function that creates a MyClass object using the (int, float) constructor
    43	  ///    // and call that function "MyClass" so that it appears as a normal constructor to the user.
    44	  ///    chai.add(constructor<MyClass (int, float)>(), "MyClass");
    45	  /// \endcode
    46	  template<typename T>
    47	  Proxy_Function constructor() {
    48	    T *f = nullptr;
    49	    return (dispatch::detail::build_constructor_(f));
    50	  }
    51	} // namespace chaiscript

Interesting! So there's already a pattern for handling non-copyable types in constructors. Now let me think about what needs to change:

The problem functions in `bootstrap_stl.hpp` are:

1. **`back_insertion_sequence_type`** (line 229-271):
   - `push_back` takes `const typename ContainerType::value_type &` - this compiles fine even for `unique_ptr` because it's just a reference. BUT - calling it requires passing a value that can be copied. However the actual problem might be that the compiler tries to instantiate the template function pointer, which forces the compiler to check if the type is complete and has the right signatures. Actually `push_back` with `const unique_ptr&` should be fine - it compiles. Let me think harder.
   
   Wait, the issue is that `void (ContainerType::*)(const typename ContainerType::value_type &)` - the function pointer type itself should be fine. But when we use `static_cast<push_back>(&ContainerType::push_back)`, the compiler instantiates this memeber function pointer type, which should be fine.

   Actually wait, let me re-read the error more carefully:
   ```
   std::unique_ptr<Foo,std::default_delete<_Ty>>::unique_ptr(const std::unique_ptr<_Ty,std::default_delete<_Ty>> &)' : attempting to reference a deleted function
   ```
   
   This error occurs in `vector` line 1708. That's in the vector's own implementation. The issue is likely that some operation requires the element type to be copyable. For example, `push_back(const T&)` itself doesn't require copying T if you only declare the pointer to it - but actually calling push_back would require copying. However, the compiler error during template instantiation might happen when you try to take the address of `push_back`.

   Actually, I think the issue is more subtle. When you have `std::vector<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>`, the vector itself is not copyable (because `unique_ptr` is not copyable). So `assignable_type` which calls `copy_constructor<ContainerType>` would fail. Also `resizable_type` takes `const typename ContainerType::value_type &val` - which would require the ability to copy a `unique_ptr` if you ever call it.

   But the key insight from the PR description is: the functions that "break unique_ptrs" are:
   - `back_insertion_sequence_type`
   - `sequence_type`  
   - `assignable_type`

   So we need to make these functions conditionally skip operations that require copyability.

Let me now write a test to reproduce the issue

I've confirmed the error. The errors come from:

1. **`back_insertion_sequence_type`**: line 249, `push_back` which takes `const value_type&` - the compiler tries to instantiate `push_back(const unique_ptr&)` which requires copying a `unique_ptr`.

2. **`resizable_type`**: line 182, `resize(n, val)` where `val` is `const value_type&` - tries to copy `unique_ptr`.

3. **`assignable_type`**: line 173-174, `copy_constructor` and `operators::assign` - both require copyability of the container (which requires copyability of the element).

4. **`sequence_type`**: line 216, `insert_at` which takes `const value_type&` - copies.

Now let me think about the solution. The approach should be to use `if constexpr` with `std::is_copy_constructible_v` to conditionally include the problematic functionality.

Now I understand the full picture. Let me look at how the workaround from the PR description changes the `vector_type` function and think about what the proper fix should be.

The PR description's workaround:
1. Comments out `back_insertion_sequence_type` 
2. Comments out `sequence_type`
3. Comments out `assignable_type`
4. Keeps `random_access_container_type`, `container_type`, `default_constructible_type`, `input_range_type`

But the proper fix should use `if constexpr` to conditionally add these features based on whether the value type is copy constructible.

Let me think about what each function needs:

1. **`assignable_type`**: calls `copy_constructor<ContainerType>` and `operators::assign<ContainerType>`. Both require the container to be copy-constructible and copy-assignable. For `std::vector<std::unique_ptr<T>>`, the vector itself is NOT copyable. So we should skip `assignable_type` if `!std::is_copy_constructible_v<ContainerType>`.

2. **`sequence_type`**: calls `insert_at` and `erase_at`. `insert_at` takes `const value_type&` - requires copyable value_type. `erase_at` is fine. So we need to conditionally add `insert_at` only if the value_type is copyable.

3. **`back_insertion_sequence_type`**: `push_back` takes `const value_type&` - requires copyable value_type. `pop_back` and `back` are fine. Also the `push_back` function pointer cast would cause the compiler to instantiate the push_back member function.

4. **`front_insertion_sequence_type`**: `push_front` takes `const_reference` - requires copyable value_type.

5. **`resizable_type`**: `resize(n, val)` takes `const value_type&` - requires copyable value_type. The single-argument `resize(n)` is fine.

Now, let me think about the best approach. Looking at the workaround, the PR suggests making a separate function `register_vector_of_unique_ptr`. But a better approach would be to use `if constexpr` to conditionally enable/disable these features.

Let me design the changes:

### 1. `assignable_type` - skip entirely if container is not copyable

```cpp
template<typename ContainerType>
void assignable_type(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    if constexpr (std::is_copy_constructible_v<ContainerType>) {
        copy_constructor<ContainerType>(type, m);
        operators::assign<ContainerType>(m);
    }
}
```

### 2. `sequence_type` - conditionally add `insert_at`

```cpp
template<typename ContainerType>
void sequence_type(const std::string & /*type*/, Module &m) {
    if constexpr (std::is_copy_constructible_v<typename ContainerType::value_type>) {
        m.add(fun(&detail::insert_at<ContainerType>), []() -> std::string {
            if (typeid(typename ContainerType::value_type) == typeid(Boxed_Value)) {
                return "insert_ref_at";
            } else {
                return "insert_at";
            }
        }());
    }
    m.add(fun(&detail::erase_at<ContainerType>), "erase_at");
}
```

    33	  /// Bidir_Range, based on the D concept of ranges.
    34	  /// \todo Update the Range code to base its capabilities on
    35	  ///       the user_typetraits of the iterator passed in
    36	  template<typename Container, typename IterType>
    37	  struct Bidir_Range {
    38	    using container_type = Container;
    39	
    40	    constexpr Bidir_Range(Container &c)
    41	        : m_begin(c.begin())
    42	        , m_end(c.end()) {
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    constexpr bool empty() const noexcept { return m_begin == m_end; }
    46	
    47	    constexpr void pop_front() {
    48	      if (empty()) {
    49	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    50	      }
    51	      ++m_begin;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    constexpr void pop_back() {
    55	      if (empty()) {
    56	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    57	      }
    58	      --m_end;
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    constexpr decltype(auto) front() const {
    62	      if (empty()) {
    63	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    64	      }
    65	      return (*m_begin);
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    constexpr decltype(auto) back() const {
    69	      if (empty()) {
    70	        throw std::range_error("Range empty");
    71	      }
    72	      auto pos = m_end;
    73	      --pos;
    74	      return (*(pos));
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    IterType m_begin;
    78	    IterType m_end;
    79	  };
    80	
    81	  namespace detail {
    82	    template<typename T>
    83	    size_t count(const T &t_target, const typename T::key_type &t_key) {
    84	      return t_target.count(t_key);
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    template<typename T>
    88	    void insert(T &t_target, const T &t_other) {
    89	      t_target.insert(t_other.begin(), t_other.end());
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    template<typename T>
    93	    void insert_ref(T &t_target, const typename T::value_type &t_val) {
    94	      t_target.insert(t_val);
    95	    }

    97	    /// Add Bidir_Range support for the given ContainerType
    98	    template<typename Bidir_Type>
    99	    void input_range_type_impl(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
   100	      m.add(user_type<Bidir_Type>(), type + "_Range");
   101	
   102	      copy_constructor<Bidir_Type>(type + "_Range", m);
   103	
   104	      m.add(constructor<Bidir_Type(typename Bidir_Type::container_type &)>(), "range_internal");
   105	
   106	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::empty), "empty");
   107	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::pop_front), "pop_front");
   108	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::front), "front");
   109	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::pop_back), "pop_back");
   110	      m.add(fun(&Bidir_Type::back), "back");
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    /// Algorithm for inserting at a specific position into a container
   114	    template<typename Type>
   115	    void insert_at(Type &container, int pos, const typename Type::value_type &v) {
   116	      auto itr = container.begin();
   117	      auto end = container.end();
   118	
   119	      if (pos < 0 || std::distance(itr, end) < pos) {
   120	        throw std::range_error("Cannot insert past end of range");
   121	      }
   122	
   123	      std::advance(itr, pos);
   124	      container.insert(itr, v);
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    /// Algorithm for erasing a specific position from a container
   128	    template<typename Type>
   129	    void erase_at(Type &container, int pos) {
   130	      auto itr = container.begin();
   131	      auto end = container.end();
   132	
   133	      if (pos < 0 || std::distance(itr, end) <= pos) {
   134	        throw std::range_error("Cannot erase past end of range");
   135	      }
   136	
   137	      std::advance(itr, pos);
   138	      container.erase(itr);
   139	    }
   140	  } // namespace detail

   152	    // In the interest of runtime safety for the m, we prefer the at() method for [] access,
   153	    // to throw an exception in an out of bounds condition.

Let me also check the `insert` function in `detail` namespace and the `unique_associative_container_type`:

Looking at line 87-90 in the original file:
```cpp
template<typename T>
void insert(T &t_target, const T &t_other) {
    t_target.insert(t_other.begin(), t_other.end());
}
```

This function copies elements from one container to another. It takes `const T &t_other` which requires the container to be copyable (since it takes a const reference to the container). But wait, that's just a reference parameter - it doesn't copy the container. The actual issue is that `t_target.insert(...)` with iterators from another container will try to copy the elements. So `insert` also requires copyable elements.

Let me check if `insert` and `insert_ref` are used only in `unique_associative_container_type`:

Line 362-370: `unique_associative_container_type` uses `detail::insert<ContainerType>` and `detail::insert_ref<ContainerType>`. The `insert` function takes `const T&` for the source container, which takes a reference (fine), but the insert operation itself copies elements. However, this is used for maps, not vectors. Let me check if maps can have non-copyable mapped types... Actually `std::map<int, std::unique_ptr<Foo>>` could also be problematic. But the PR description focuses on vectors.

Let me also check if there's an issue with `insert_ref` at line 92-95:
```cpp
template<typename T>
void insert_ref(T &t_target, const typename T::value_type &t_val) {
    t_target.insert(t_val);
}
```
This takes a const reference to the value_type and inserts it - that requires copying the element. So for non-copyable mapped types, this would also fail.

However, the PR description is specifically about `std::vector<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>`. Let me focus on making the minimal changes to satisfy the PR description. The `unique_associative_container_type` is used for maps, and if someone uses a map with non-copyable elements, they'd hit similar issues, but that's a separate concern.

#include "chaiscript/chaiscript.hpp"
#include "chaiscript/chaiscript_stdlib.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <memory>
#include <iostream>

struct Foo {
    int x;
    Foo(int val) : x(val) {}
};

int main() {
    chaiscript::ChaiScript chai;
    
    // Register the vector type
    chai.add(chaiscript::user_type<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>(), "FooPtr");
    
    auto module = chaiscript::ModulePtr(new chaiscript::Module());
    chaiscript::bootstrap::standard_library::vector_type<std::vector<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>>("FooPtrVector", *module);
    chai.add(module);
    
    // Now also test with a list
    auto module2 = chaiscript::ModulePtr(new chaiscript::Module());
    chaiscript::bootstrap::standard_library::list_type<std::list<std::unique_ptr<Foo>>>("FooPtrList", *module2);
    chai.add(module2);
    
    std::cout << "Compilation successful!" << std::endl;
    return 0;
}

```cpp
template<typename PairType>
void pair_type(const std::string &type, Module &m) {
    m.add(user_type<PairType>(), type);
    m.add(fun(&PairType::first), "first");
    m.add(fun(&PairType::second), "second");
    basic_constructors<PairType>(type, m);  // This adds copy constructor!
    m.add(constructor<PairType(const typename PairType::first_type &, const typename PairType::second_type &)>(), type);
}
```

The `basic_constructors` function adds a copy constructor for the pair. And also the two-argument constructor takes const references to the element types. Both of these would fail for non-copyable elements.

I notice that there's a prelude function `insert_at` defined at `chaiscript_prelude.hpp:133` that calls `insert_ref_at`. But this is a chaiscript function, and it would only be called if the user invokes `insert_at` on a container. Since we've guarded `insert_at`/`insert_ref_at` registration for non-copyable types, this prelude function won't be able to call `insert_ref_at` on those containers (because the method won't exist). That's the correct behavior.
